            }

            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("trb_ad_300x600/300x250_1_/");
                oVa["trb_ad_300x600/300x250_1_/"] = ["NULL"];
              } else {
                oPageUnload('trb_ad_300x600/300x250_1_/', true);
              }
            }
          
          function loadAd() {
            dfpService.appendAd({
              id: 'hp_745',
              optimeraId: 'trb_ad_300x600/300x250_1_/',
              adType: 'cube',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.nydn/hp',
              displayMobile: true,
              displayDesktop: true,
              isOOP: false,
              is5x1: false,
              dimensionsString: '[[300, 600], [300, 250]]',
              sizemapString: '',
              sizemapRefresh: 'false',
              refreshOnPhotoChange: false,
              adRefreshInterval: 0,
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true,
              loadImmediately: true
            }, false, true)
          }
          loadAd();
        
      }
    })()
            </script>
           </div>

             <h2>
              <a aria-describedby="headline-210" class="feature-header tag width-100 flex-container-row" data-pb-field="customFeatureHeaderText" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="spring cleaning" data-tr-content-id="202004211100TMS_____ACTVTISL_F704CDE4135B2E2A7B679903A05B87F_slideshow" href="/featured/sns-cleaning-tips-from-professional-cleaners-20200508-njiiq2p5jnaqnle236ioeathhq-photogallery.html" style="color: #000; border-bottom: 4px solid #000;" tabindex="-1">
               spring cleaning
              </a>

             <div class="crd--cnt align-items-start flex-container-column">

                 </a>
                </h3>
               </div>
               <div class="preview-text spaced spaced-top story-preview spaced-md hddn-mble hddn-dktp hddn-tbl hddn-mble" data-pb-field="description.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here.">
                Almost all of us are spending a lot of time at home, which may mean spring cleaning, tidying up and wiping stuff down like weve never done before.                 <a class="no-u" data-pb-field="headlines.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write headline here" data-pb-url-field="canonical_url" data-tr-content-id="FET42O7TGBH4XG5FSBIQMV53GM" href="/national-sports/sns-rnkr-march-madness-facts-you-ve-never-heard-before-20190320-photogallery.html" id="headline-1456">

                </a>
               </h3>
              </div>
              <div class="preview-text spaced spaced-top story-preview spaced-md hddn-mble hddn-dktp hddn-tbl hddn-mble" data-pb-field="description.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here.">
               The NCAA Men's Basketball tournament isn't called "March Madness" for nothing. It's one of the most prominent events in American sports, generating more than a billion dollars, legendary performances, and, of course, interesting facts. From its humble beginnings with teams competing for a second-rate championship, it's grown into an entire month of college basketball mania. The history of the tournament is rich with exciting anecdotes and all manner of March Madness trivia. NCAA tournament history goes way beyond sheer numbers and rote lists of upsets. For example, did you know the now-basement dwelling National Invitation Tournament (NIT) was once actually a bigger deal than the Big Dance? Or that gambling brought down one of the greatest teams in college basketball history, and kept the tournament out of New York for six decades? Or that men getting snipped in time to watch the early rounds has become a popular trend? These March Madness facts might surprise you. Visit
               <a href="https://www.ranker.com/" target="_blank">
                Ranker.com
               </a>
               for similar lists and rankings.
